```python
group_data = df.groupby("depression_label").mean(numeric_only=True)
group_data["stress_level"].plot(kind="bar")

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
plt.title("Stress Level: Depressed vs Not Depressed")
plt.xlabel("Depression Label (0 = No, 1 = Yes)")
plt.ylabel("Average Stress Level")
plt.show()
```

```python
# =========================================
# 1. Social Media vs Stress (LINE → TREND)
# =========================================
plt.figure()
df.groupby("daily_social_media_hours")["stress_level"].mean().plot(marker='o')
plt.title("Does Social Media Increase Stress?")
plt.xlabel("Daily Social Media Hours")
plt.ylabel("Average Stress Level")
plt.grid()
plt.show()
```

```python
depressed_df = df[df["depression_label"] == 1]
```


```python
low_sleep = (depressed_df["sleep_hours"] < 6).sum()
```


```python
high_social = (depressed_df["daily_social_media_hours"] > 5).sum()
```


```python
low_academic = depressed_df[
    depressed_df["academic_performance"].isin(["Low","Poor"])
].shape[0]
```


```python
total = len(depressed_df)

print("Total depressed:", total)
print("Low sleep (<6 hrs):", low_sleep)
print("High social media (>5 hrs):", high_social)
print("Low academic performance:", low_academic)
```

    Total depressed: 31
    Low sleep (<6 hrs): 31
    High social media (>5 hrs): 31
    Low academic performance: 0

```python
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

labels = ["Low Sleep", "High Social Media", "Low Academic"]
values = [low_sleep, high_social, low_academic]
```

```python
import pandas as pd

depressed_df["academic_group"] = pd.cut(
    depressed_df["academic_performance"],
    bins=[0,2.5,3.5,5],
    labels=["Low","Medium","High"]
)
```
